# User Requirement
Please design a user interface (UI) feature for a website or application based on the following requirement.

1.  **Core Objective:** Implement a dedicated, separate scrollbar for a navigation area (nav) within the interface.

2.  **Detailed Requirements:**
    *   The scrollbar must be visually distinct from any main content or global scrollbar.
    *   It should control scrolling *only* within the boundaries of the navigation panel.
    *   The navigation content should become scrollable only when its content height exceeds the available vertical space of the nav container.

3.  **Functional Specifications:**
    *   **Trigger:** The separate scrollbar must appear automatically when the navigation content overflows its container.
    *   **Behavior:** The scrollbar must allow smooth vertical scrolling of the navigation items.
    *   **Scope:** Scrolling via this nav scrollbar must not affect the position of any other page elements or the main window's scroll position.

4.  **Design & Usability Considerations:**
    *   **Visibility:** The scrollbar should be clearly visible and accessible to users.
    *   **Styling:** Provide suggestions for styling (e.g., color, width, hover effects) to ensure it matches the overall design theme while remaining functionally clear.
    *   **Platform Consistency:** Consider operating system conventions (e.g., overlay scrollbars on macOS vs. persistent scrollbars on Windows) if relevant.

Please provide a technical implementation approach (e.g., using CSS `overflow` properties) along with a brief visual mockup or description of the styled component.

     1 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     2 
     3 // Convert base64 string to Uint8Array for VAPID key
     4 function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String: string) {
     5   const padding = '='.repeat((4 - (base64String.length % 4)) % 4);
     6   const base64 = (base64String + padding).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
     7   const rawData = window.atob(base64);
     8   const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);
     9   for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) {
    10     outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
    11   }
    12   return outputArray;
    13 }
    14 
    15 export async function subscribeToPush(userId: string) {
    16   if (!('serviceWorker' in navigator) || !('PushManager' in window)) {
    17     throw new Error('Push notifications are not supported in this browser');
    18   }
    19 
    20   const registration = await navigator.serviceWorker.ready;
    21 
    22   // Get VAPID public key from settings or a known place
    23   // For simplicity, we assume it's available in an env var or we fetch it
    24   const { data: settings } = await supabase
    25     .from('settings')
    26     .select('*')
    27     .in('key', ['vapid_public_key', 'vapid_subject']) as { data: any[] | null };
    28 
    29   const publicVapidKey = settings?.find((s: any) => s.key === 'vapid_public_key')?.value || import.meta.env.VITE_VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY;
    30   // const vapidSubject = settings?.find((s: any) => s.key === 'vapid_subject')?.value || 'mailto:info@goldxusdt.com';
    31 
    32   if (!publicVapidKey) {
    33     throw new Error('VAPID public key not found');
    34   }
    35 
    36   const subscription = await registration.pushManager.subscribe({
    37     userVisibleOnly: true,
    38     applicationServerKey: urlBase64ToUint8Array(publicVapidKey)
    39   });
    40 
    41   // Save subscription to database
    42   const { error } = await supabase.from('push_subscriptions').upsert({
    43     user_id: userId,
    44     subscription_json: subscription.toJSON(),
    45     updated_at: new Date().toISOString()
    46   } as any, { onConflict: 'user_id' });
    47 
    48   if (error) throw error;
    49 
    50   return subscription;
    51 }
    52 
    53 export async function unsubscribeFromPush(userId: string) {
    54   if (!('serviceWorker' in navigator)) return;
    55 
    56   const registration = await navigator.serviceWorker.ready;
    57   const subscription = await registration.pushManager.getSubscription();
    58 
    59   if (subscription) {
    60     await subscription.unsubscribe();
    61   }
    62 
    63   const { error } = await supabase
    64     .from('push_subscriptions')
    65     .delete()
    66     .eq('user_id', userId);
    67 
    68   if (error) throw error;
    69 }
    70 
    71 export async function getSubscriptionData(userId: string) {
    72   const { data, error } = await supabase
    73     .from('push_subscriptions')
    74     .select('*')
    75     .eq('user_id', userId)
    76     .maybeSingle();
    77 
    78   if (error) throw error;
    79   return data;
    80 }
    81 
    82 export async function updateSubscriptionPreferences(userId: string, categories: string[]) {
    83   const { error } = await supabase
    84     .from('push_subscriptions')
    85     // @ts-ignore
    86     .update({ categories })
    87     .eq('user_id', userId);
    88 
    89   if (error) throw error;
    90 }
    91 
    92 export async function getSubscriptionStatus(userId: string) {
    93   const data = await getSubscriptionData(userId);
    94   return !!data;
    95 }
    96 
    97 export function registerServiceWorker() {
    98   if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
    99     window.addEventListener('load', () => {
   100       navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js').then(
   101         (registration) => {
   102           console.log('ServiceWorker registration successful with scope: ', registration.scope);
   103         },
   104         (err) => {
   105           console.log('ServiceWorker registration failed: ', err);
   106         }
   107       );
   108     });
   109   }

    70 export default function AdvancedReferralPage() {
    71   const { user } = useAuth();
    72   const navigate = useNavigate();
    73   const [downline, setDownline] = useState<DownlineUser[]>([]);
    74   const [stats, setStats] = useState<CommissionStat[]>([]);
    75   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    76   const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
    77   const [levelFilter, setLevelFilter] = useState('all');
    78   const [expandedNodes, setExpandedNodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
    79 
    80   useEffect(() => {
    81     if (user) {
    82       loadData();
    83     }
    84   }, [user]);
    85 
    86   const loadData = async () => {
    87     if (!user) return;
    88     setLoading(true);
    89     try {
    90       const { data: downlineData, error: downlineError } = await (supabase.rpc as any)('get_downline_network', { 
    91         p_user_id: user.id 
    92       });
    93 
    94       if (downlineError) throw downlineError;
    95 
    96       const { data: statsData, error: statsError } = await (supabase.rpc as any)('get_referral_commission_stats', { 
    97         p_user_id: user.id 
    98       });
    99 
   100       if (statsError) throw statsError;
   101 
   102       setDownline(downlineData || []);
   103       setStats(statsData || []);
   104     } catch (error) {
   105       console.error('Failed to load referral data:', error);
   106       toast.error('Failed to load referral data');
   107     } finally {
   108       setLoading(false);
   109     }
   110   };
   111 
   112   const toggleNode = (userId: string) => {
   113     const newExpanded = new Set(expandedNodes);
   114     if (newExpanded.has(userId)) {
   115       newExpanded.delete(userId);
   116     } else {
   117       newExpanded.add(userId);
   118     }
   119     setExpandedNodes(newExpanded);
   120   };
   121 
   122   const buildTree = (users: DownlineUser[]) => {
   123     const userMap = new Map<string, DownlineUser>();
   124     const rootNodes: DownlineUser[] = [];
   125 
   126     // Initialize all nodes
   127     users.forEach(u => {
   128       userMap.set(u.user_id, { ...u, children: [] });
   129     });
   130 
   131     // Link nodes to their parents
   132     users.forEach(u => {
   133       const node = userMap.get(u.user_id)!;
   134       if (u.referrer_id === user?.id) {
   135         rootNodes.push(node);
   136       } else {
   137         const parent = userMap.get(u.referrer_id);
   138         if (parent) {
   139           parent.children?.push(node);
   140         }
   141       }
   142     });
   143 
   144     return rootNodes;
   145   };
   146 
   147   const filteredDownline = downline.filter(u => {
   148     const matchesSearch = u.username?.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||

   150     const matchesLevel = levelFilter === 'all' || u.level === parseInt(levelFilter);
   151     return matchesSearch && matchesLevel;

   196   const TreeNode = ({ node, level = 0 }: { node: DownlineUser; level?: number }) => {

     1 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION get_downline_network(p_user_id UUID, p_max_levels INTEGER DEFAULT 15)
     2 RETURNS TABLE (
     3   user_id UUID,
     4   username TEXT,
     5   email TEXT,
     6   level INTEGER,
     7   referrer_id UUID,
     8   created_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
     9   kyc_status public.kyc_status,
    10   is_active BOOLEAN
    11 ) AS $$
    12 BEGIN
    13   RETURN QUERY
    14   WITH RECURSIVE downline AS (
    15     -- Initial base case (direct referrals)
    16     SELECT 
    17       p.id as user_id, 
    18       p.username, 
    19       p.email, 
    20       1 as level, 
    21       p.referrer_id, 
    22       p.created_at, 
    23       p.kyc_status, 
    24       p.is_active
    25     FROM profiles p
    26     WHERE p.referrer_id = p_user_id
    27     
    28     UNION ALL
    29     
    30     -- Recursive step
    31     SELECT 
    32       p.id, 
    33       p.username, 
    34       p.email, 
    35       d.level + 1, 
    36       p.referrer_id, 
    37       p.created_at, 
    38       p.kyc_status, 
    39       p.is_active
    40     FROM profiles p
    41     INNER JOIN downline d ON p.referrer_id = d.user_id
    42     WHERE d.level < p_max_levels
    43   )
    44   SELECT * FROM downline;
    45 END;
    46 $$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;
    47 
    48 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION get_referral_commission_stats(p_user_id UUID)
    49 RETURNS TABLE (
    50   level INTEGER,
    51   total_commission DECIMAL(20, 8),
    52   member_count INTEGER,
    53   commission_rate DECIMAL(20, 8)
    54 ) AS $$
    55 BEGIN
    56   RETURN QUERY
    57   WITH RECURSIVE downline AS (
    58     -- Initial base case
    59     SELECT p.id, 1 as level
    60     FROM profiles p
    61     WHERE p.referrer_id = p_user_id
    62     
    63     UNION ALL
    64     
    65     -- Recursive step
    66     SELECT p.id, d.level + 1
    67     FROM profiles p
    68     INNER JOIN downline d ON p.referrer_id = d.user_id
    69     WHERE d.level < 15
    70   ),
    71   stats AS (
    72     SELECT 
    73       d.level,
    74       COALESCE(SUM(rc.commission_amount), 0) as total_commission,
    75       COUNT(DISTINCT d.id) as member_count
    76     FROM downline d
    77     LEFT JOIN referral_commissions rc ON rc.referred_user_id = d.id AND rc.referrer_id = p_user_id AND rc.level = d.level
    78     GROUP BY d.level
    79   )
    80   SELECT 
    81     s.level,
    82     s.total_commission,
    83     s.member_count,
    84     (SELECT (COALESCE(value, '0')::DECIMAL / 100.0)
    85      FROM settings 
    86      WHERE key = 'level' || s.level || '_commission'
    87         OR key = 'referral_level' || s.level || '_commission'
    88         OR key = 'referral_level' || s.level || '_percentage'
    89      ORDER BY (
    90        CASE 
    91          WHEN key = 'level' || s.level || '_commission' THEN 1
    92          WHEN key = 'referral_level' || s.level || '_commission' THEN 2
    93          ELSE 3
    94        END
    95      ) ASC
    96      LIMIT 1) as commission_rate
    97   FROM stats s
    98   ORDER BY s.level ASC;
    99 END;
   100 $$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;

```
function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String: string) {
  const padding = '='.repeat((4 - (base64String.length % 4)) % 4);
  const base64 = (base64String + padding).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
  const rawData = window.atob(base64);
  const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) {
    outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
  }
  return outputArray;
}

```
New String: ```
function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String: string) {
  const padding = '='.repeat((4 - (base64String.length % 4)) % 4);
  const base64 = (base64String + padding).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
  const rawData = window.atob(base64);
  const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) {
    outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
  }

  // If the key is in DER format (SubjectPublicKeyInfo), extract the raw 65-byte public key
  // Raw uncompressed P-256 public key starts with 0x04 and is 65 bytes long
  if (outputArray.length > 65) {
    return outputArray.slice(-65);
  }

  return outputArray;
}

```

    35       }
    36       setThreshold(profile?.balance_threshold?.toString() || '0');
    37     } catch (error) {
    38       console.error('Error loading notification data:', error);
    39     } finally {
    40       setLoading(false);
    41     }
    42   };
    43 
    44   const handleToggleSubscription = async () => {
    45     if (!user) return;
    46     setActionLoading(true);
    47     try {
    48       if (isSubscribed) {
    49         await unsubscribeFromPush(user.id);
    50         setIsSubscribed(false);
    51         setCategories([]);
    52         toast.success('Unsubscribed from push notifications');
    53       } else {
    54         await subscribeToPush(user.id);
    55         setIsSubscribed(true);
    56         // Default categories
    57         const defaultCats = ['announcements', 'account', 'roi_arrival', 'balance_threshold'];
    58         await updateSubscriptionPreferences(user.id, defaultCats);
    59         setCategories(defaultCats);
    60         toast.success('Successfully subscribed to push notifications!');
    61       }
    62     } catch (error: any) {
    63       console.error('Subscription error:', error);
    64       toast.error(error.message || 'Failed to update subscription');
    65     } finally {
    66       setActionLoading(false);
    67     }
    68   };
    69 
    70   const handleToggleCategory = async (catId: string) => {
    71     if (!user || !isSubscribed) return;
    72     
    73     const newCats = categories.includes(catId) 
    74       ? categories.filter(c => c !== catId)
    75       : [...categories, catId];
    76     
    77     try {
    78       await updateSubscriptionPreferences(user.id, newCats);
    79       setCategories(newCats);
    80       toast.success('Preference updated');
    81     } catch (error) {
    82       toast.error('Failed to update preference');
    83     }
    84   };
    85 
    86   const handleSaveThreshold = async () => {
    87     if (!user) return;
    88     setActionLoading(true);
    89     try {
    90       const val = parseFloat(threshold);
    91       if (isNaN(val) || val < 0) {
    92         toast.error('Please enter a valid amount');
    93         return;
    94       }
    95       await updateProfile(user.id, { balance_threshold: val });
    96       toast.success('Balance threshold updated');
    97     } catch (error) {
    98       toast.error('Failed to update threshold');
    99     } finally {
   100       setActionLoading(false);
   101     }
   102   };
   103 
   104   if (loading) {
   105     return (
   106       <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-[60vh]">
   107         <Loader2 className="h-10 w-10 animate-spin text-primary" />
   108       </div>
   109     );
   110   }
   111 
   112   return (
   113     <div className="p-4 sm:p-6 lg:p-10 space-y-8 max-w-4xl mx-auto">
   114       <SEOHead title="Notification Preferences" noindex={true} />
   115       
   116       <div className="space-y-1">
   117         <h1 className="text-2xl sm:text-4xl font-black v56-gradient-text tracking-tight leading-tight flex items-center gap-3">
   118           <Bell className="h-8 w-8 text-primary" />
   119           Notification <span className="text-foreground">Preferences</span>
   120         </h1>
   121         <p className="text-xs uppercase font-bold tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">
   122           Manage how you receive updates and alerts
   123         </p>
   124       </div>
   125 
   126       <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-6">
   127         <Card className="v56-glass premium-border overflow-hidden">
   128           <CardHeader className="bg-primary/5 border-b border-white/5">
   129             <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
   130               <div className="space-y-1">
   131                 <CardTitle className="text-lg font-black flex items-center gap-2">
   132                   <Smartphone className="h-5 w-5 text-primary" />
   133                   Browser Push Notifications
   134                 </CardTitle>
   135                 <CardDescription>
   136                   Receive real-time updates directly in your browser.
   137                 </CardDescription>
   138               </div>
   139               <Badge variant={isSubscribed ? "default" : "outline"} className={isSubscribed ? "bg-green-500/20 text-green-500 hover:bg-green-500/30" : ""}>
   140                 {isSubscribed ? 'Subscribed' : 'Not Subscribed'}
   141               </Badge>
   142             </div>
   143           </CardHeader>
   144           <CardContent className="p-6 space-y-6">
   145             <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 rounded-2xl bg-white/5 border border-white/10 transition-colors hover:bg-white/10">
   146               <div className="space-y-0.5">
   147                 <Label className="text-sm font-bold">Enable Push Notifications</Label>
   148                 <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Get notified about blog posts, announcements, and account activity.</p>
   149               </div>
   150               <Switch 
   151                 checked={isSubscribed} 
   152                 onCheckedChange={handleToggleSubscription}
   153                 disabled={actionLoading}
   154               />
   155             </div>
   156 
   157             <div className="space-y-4">
   158               <h3 className="text-xs font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">Notification Categories</h3>
   159               
   160               <div className="space-y-3">
   161                 {[
   162                   { id: 'announcements', label: 'System Announcements', desc: 'Major platform updates and news' },
   163                   { id: 'blog', label: 'New Blog Posts', desc: 'Stay updated with our latest articles' },
   164                   { id: 'account', label: 'Account Activity', desc: 'Security alerts and transaction updates' },
   165                   { id: 'roi_arrival', label: 'ROI Arrival', desc: 'Get notified as soon as ROI is credited' },
   166                   { id: 'balance_threshold', label: 'Balance Threshold', desc: 'Alert when your total balance reaches a target' },
   167                 ].map((category) => (
   168                   <div key={category.id} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 rounded-xl bg-white/5 border border-white/5">
   169                     <div className="space-y-0.5">
   170                       <Label className="text-xs font-bold">{category.label}</Label>
   171                       <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{category.desc}</p>
   172                     </div>
   173                     <Switch 
   174                       checked={categories.includes(category.id)} 
   175                       onCheckedChange={() => handleToggleCategory(category.id)}
   176                       disabled={!isSubscribed} 
   177                     />
   178                   </div>
   179                 ))}
   180               </div>
   181             </div>
   182 
   183             <div className="space-y-4 p-4 rounded-2xl bg-white/5 border border-white/10">
   184               <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-2">
   185                 <TrendingUp className="h-5 w-5 text-green-500" />
   186                 <div className="space-y-0.5">
   187                   <Label className="text-sm font-bold">Balance Alert Threshold</Label>
   188                   <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground italic">Set a value to receive an alert when your total balance reaches it.</p>
   189                 </div>
   190               </div>
   191               
   192               <div className="flex gap-3">
   193                 <div className="relative flex-1 group">
   194                   <div className="absolute inset-y-0 left-0 pl-3 flex items-center pointer-events-none text-muted-foreground group-focus-within:text-primary transition-colors">
   195                     <Wallet size={14} />

   197                   <Input 
   198                     type="number"

   212                 >
   213                   {actionLoading ? 'Saving...' : 'Set Threshold'}
   214                 </Button>
   215               </div>
   216             </div>
   217 
   218             {isSubscribed && (

   227           </CardContent>
   228         </Card>
   229

     1 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     2 
     3 // Convert base64 string to Uint8Array for VAPID key
     4 function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String: string) {
     5   const padding = '='.repeat((4 - (base64String.length % 4)) % 4);
     6   const base64 = (base64String + padding).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
     7   const rawData = window.atob(base64);
     8   const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);
     9   for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) {
    10     outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
    11   }
    12 
    13   // If the key is in DER format (SubjectPublicKeyInfo), extract the raw 65-byte public key
    14   // Raw uncompressed P-256 public key starts with 0x04 and is 65 bytes long
    15   if (outputArray.length > 65) {
    16     return outputArray.slice(-65);
    17   }
    18 
    19   return outputArray;
    20 }
    21 
    22 export async function subscribeToPush(userId: string) {
    23   if (!('serviceWorker' in navigator) || !('PushManager' in window)) {
    24     throw new Error('Push notifications are not supported in this browser');
    25   }
    26 
    27   const registration = await navigator.serviceWorker.ready;
    28 
    29   // Get VAPID public key from settings or a known place
    30   // For simplicity, we assume it's available in an env var or we fetch it
    31   const { data: settings } = await supabase
    32     .from('settings')
    33     .select('*')
    34     .in('key', ['vapid_public_key', 'vapid_subject']) as { data: any[] | null };
    35 
    36   const publicVapidKey = settings?.find((s: any) => s.key === 'vapid_public_key')?.value || import.meta.env.VITE_VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY;
    37   // const vapidSubject = settings?.find((s: any) => s.key === 'vapid_subject')?.value || 'mailto:info@goldxusdt.com';
    38 
    39   if (!publicVapidKey) {
    40     throw new Error('VAPID public key not found');
    41   }
    42 
    43   const subscription = await registration.pushManager.subscribe({
    44     userVisibleOnly: true,
    45     applicationServerKey: urlBase64ToUint8Array(publicVapidKey)
    46   });
    47 
    48   // Save subscription to database
    49   const { error } = await supabase.from('push_subscriptions').upsert({
    50     user_id: userId,
    51     subscription_json: subscription.toJSON(),
    52     updated_at: new Date().toISOString()
    53   } as any, { onConflict: 'user_id' });
    54 
    55   if (error) throw error;
    56 
    57   return subscription;
    58 }
    59 
    60 export async function unsubscribeFromPush(userId: string) {
    61   if (!('serviceWorker' in navigator)) return;
    62 
    63   const registration = await navigator.serviceWorker.ready;
    64   const subscription = await registration.pushManager.getSubscription();
    65 
    66   if (subscription) {
    67     await subscription.unsubscribe();
    68   }
    69 
    70   const { error } = await supabase
    71     .from('push_subscriptions')
    72     .delete()
    73     .eq('user_id', userId);
    74 
    75   if (error) throw error;
    76 }
    77 
    78 export async function getSubscriptionData(userId: string) {
    79   const { data, error } = await supabase
    80     .from('push_subscriptions')
    81     .select('*')
    82     .eq('user_id', userId)
    83     .maybeSingle();
    84 
    85   if (error) throw error;
    86   return data;
    87 }
    88 
    89 export async function updateSubscriptionPreferences(userId: string, categories: string[]) {
    90   const { error } = await supabase
    91     .from('push_subscriptions')
    92     // @ts-ignore
    93     .update({ categories })
    94     .eq('user_id', userId);
    95 
    96   if (error) throw error;
    97 }
    98 
    99 export async function getSubscriptionStatus(userId: string) {
   100   const data = await getSubscriptionData(userId);
   101   return !!data;
   102 }
   103 
   104 export function registerServiceWorker() {
   105   if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
   106     window.addEventListener('load', () => {
   107       navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js').then(
   108         (registration) => {
   109           console.log('ServiceWorker registration successful with scope: ', registration.scope);
   110         },
   111         (err) => {
   112           console.log('ServiceWorker registration failed: ', err);
   113         }
   114       );
   115     });
   116   }

    35 // Profile operations
    36 export async function getProfile(userId: string): Promise<Profile | null> {
    37   const { data, error } = await supabase
    38     .from('profiles')
    39     .select('*')
    40     .eq('id', userId)
    41     .maybeSingle();
    42 
    43   if (error) {
    44     console.error('Error fetching profile:', error);
    45     return null;
    46   }
    47   return data;
    48 }

    50 /**
    51  * Helper to check balance threshold and ROI arrival and send push notifications
    52  */
    53 export async function checkAndSendAutomatedNotifications(userId: string, eventType: 'roi_arrival' | 'balance_threshold', amount?: number) {
    54   try {
    55     const { data: profile } = await supabase
    56       .from('profiles')
    57       .select('balance_threshold, last_balance_alert_at')
    58       .eq('id', userId)
    59       .single();
    60 
    61     if (!profile) return;
    62 
    63     if (eventType === 'roi_arrival') {
    64       await invokeEdgeFunction('send-push-notification', {
    65         body: {
    66           target_type: 'individual',
    67           target_id: userId,
    68           category: 'roi_arrival',
    69           title: 'ROI Received 💰',
    70           body: `You have received ${amount} USDT in ROI credits!`,
    71           action_url: '/transactions'
    72         }
    73       });
    74     }
    75 
    76     if (eventType === 'balance_threshold') {
    77       const balances = await getWalletBalances(userId);
    78       const threshold = Number(profile.balance_threshold);
    79       const lastAlert = profile.last_balance_alert_at;
    80       const oneHourAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 3600000);
    81 
    82       if (threshold > 0 && balances.total >= threshold && (!lastAlert || new Date(lastAlert) < oneHourAgo)) {
    83         await updateProfile(userId, { last_balance_alert_at: new Date().toISOString() });
    84         await invokeEdgeFunction('send-push-notification', {
    85           body: {
    86             target_type: 'individual',
    87             target_id: userId,
    88             category: 'balance_threshold',
    89             title: 'Balance Alert ⚖️',
    90             body: `Your total balance has reached your threshold of ${threshold} USDT! Current balance: ${balances.total} USDT.`,
    91             action_url: '/dashboard'
    92           }
    93         });
    94       }
    95     }
    96   } catch (err) {
    97     console.error('Error in automated notifications:', err);
    98   }

   126 // Wallet operations
   127 export async function getWalletBalances(userId: string): Promise<WalletBalances> {
   128   const { data, error } = await supabase
   129     .from('wallets')
   130     .select('wallet_type, balance')
   131     .eq('user_id', userId);
   132 
   133   if (error || !data) {
   134     console.error('Error fetching wallet balances:', error);
   135     return { deposit: 0, roi: 0, bonus: 0, withdrawal: 0, total: 0 };
   136   }
   137 
   138   const balances: WalletBalances = {
   139     deposit: 0,
   140     roi: 0,
   141     bonus: 0,
   142     withdrawal: 0,
   143     total: 0
   144   };
   145 
   146   data.forEach((wallet) => {
   147     const balance = Number(wallet.balance);
   148     balances[wallet.wallet_type as keyof Omit<WalletBalances, 'total'>] = balance;
   149     balances.total += balance;
   150   });
   151 
   152   return balances;
   153 }

   199 // Deposit operations
   200 export async function createDeposit(
   201   userId: string,
   202   amount: number,
   203   network: NetworkType,
   204   transactionHash: string,
   205   couponId?: string,
   206   couponBonus: number = 0
   207 ) {
   208   const fee = amount * 0.05; // 5% fee
   209   const netAmount = amount - fee;
   210 
   211   // Create transaction record
   212   const { data: transaction, error: txError } = await supabase
   213     .from('transactions')
   214     .insert({
   215       user_id: userId,
   216       transaction_type: 'deposit',
   217       amount,
   218       fee,
   219       net_amount: netAmount + couponBonus, // Final amount user gets
   220       status: 'pending',
   221       network,
   222       transaction_hash: transactionHash
   223     })
   224     .select()
   225     .single();
   226 
   227   if (txError || !transaction) {
   228     return { data: null, error: txError };
   229   }
   230 
   231   // Create deposit record
   232   const { data, error } = await supabase
   233     .from('deposits')
   234     .insert({
   235       transaction_id: transaction.id,
   236       user_id: userId,
   237       amount,
   238       fee,
   239       net_amount: netAmount + couponBonus,
   240       network,
   241       transaction_hash: transactionHash,
   242       status: 'pending',
   243       coupon_id: couponId || null,
   244       coupon_bonus: couponBonus
   245     })
   246     .select()
   247     .single();
   248 
   249   return { data, error };
   250 }
   251

   284 export async function approveDeposit(depositId: string, adminId: string) {
   285   const { data, error } = await supabase.rpc('process_deposit_approval', {
   286     deposit_id_param: depositId,
   287     admin_id: adminId
   288   });
   289 
   290   if (!error) {
   291     // Get user_id to check threshold
   292     const { data: dep } = await supabase.from('deposits').select('user_id').eq('id', depositId).single();
   293     if (dep) {
   294       checkAndSendAutomatedNotifications(dep.user_id, 'balance_threshold');
   295     }
   296   }
   297 
   298   return { data, error };
   299 }

   301 export async function rejectDeposit(depositId: string, adminNotes: string) {
   302   const { data: deposit, error: depositError } = await supabase
   303     .from('deposits')
   304     .select('transaction_id')
   305     .eq('id', depositId)
   306     .maybeSingle();
   307 
   308   if (depositError || !deposit) {
   309     return { data: null, error: depositError };
   310   }
   311 
   312   // Update deposit status
   313   await supabase
   314     .from('deposits')
   315     .update({ status: 'rejected' })
   316     .eq('id', depositId);
   317 
   318   // Update transaction status
   319   const { data, error } = await supabase
   320     .from('transactions')
   321     .update({ status: 'rejected', admin_notes: adminNotes })
   322     .eq('id', deposit.transaction_id)
   323     .select()
   324     .maybeSingle();
   325 
   326   return { data, error };
   327 }

   329 // Withdrawal operations
   330 export async function createWithdrawal(
   331   userId: string,
   332   amount: number,
   333   walletAddress: string,
   334   network: NetworkType,
   335   isReferralBonus: boolean
   336 ) {
   337   const fee = amount * 0.05; // 5% fee
   338   const netAmount = amount - fee;
   339   const coolingPeriod = isReferralBonus ? 30 : 2; // 30 days for referral bonus, 2 days for normal
   340   const coolingPeriodEnd = new Date();
   341   coolingPeriodEnd.setDate(coolingPeriodEnd.getDate() + coolingPeriod);
   342 
   343   // Create transaction record
   344   const { data: transaction, error: txError } = await supabase
   345     .from('transactions')
   346     .insert({
   347       user_id: userId,
   348       transaction_type: 'withdrawal',
   349       amount,
   350       fee,
   351       net_amount: netAmount,
   352       status: 'pending',
   353       network,
   354       wallet_address: walletAddress
   355     })
   356     .select()
   357     .single();
   358 
   359   if (txError || !transaction) {
   360     return { data: null, error: txError };
   361   }
   362 
   363   // Deduct balance from wallet
   364   const sourceWallet = isReferralBonus ? 'bonus' : 'roi';
   365   const { error: walletError } = await supabase.rpc('deduct_wallet_balance', {
   366     p_user_id: userId,
   367     p_wallet_type: sourceWallet,
   368     p_amount: amount
   369   });
   370 
   371   if (walletError) {
   372     // Cleanup transaction on failure
   373     await supabase.from('transactions').delete().eq('id', transaction.id);
   374     return { data: null, error: walletError };
   375   }
   376 
   377   // Create withdrawal record
   378   const { data, error } = await supabase
   379     .from('withdrawals')
   380     .insert({
   381       transaction_id: transaction.id,
   382       user_id: userId,
   383       amount,
   384       fee,
   385       net_amount: netAmount,
   386       wallet_address: walletAddress,
   387       network,
   388       status: 'pending',
   389       cooling_period_end: coolingPeriodEnd.toISOString(),
   390       is_referral_bonus: isReferralBonus
   391     })
   392     .select()
   393     .single();
   394 
   395   if (error) {
   396     // Refund wallet if withdrawal record creation fails
   397     await supabase.rpc('add_wallet_balance', {
   398       p_user_id: userId,
   399       p_wallet_type: sourceWallet,
   400       p_amount: amount
   401     });
   402     await supabase.from('transactions').delete().eq('id', transaction.id);
   403     return { error };
   404   }
   405 
   406   // Trigger Telegram Alert
   407   invokeEdgeFunction('send-telegram-alert', {
   408     body: {
   409       event_type: 'withdrawal_request',
   410       title: 'New Withdrawal Request',
   411       details: `User ID: ${userId}\nAmount: ${amount} USDT\nNetwork: ${network}`,
   412       record: { id: (data as any).id }
   413     }
   414   }).catch(err => console.error('Telegram alert failed:', err));
   415 
   416   // Check balance threshold
   417   checkAndSendAutomatedNotifications(userId, 'balance_threshold');
   418 
   419   return { data, error };
   420 }
   421 
   422 export async function getLeaderboard(limit = 5) {
   423   const { data, error } = await supabase
   424     .from('profiles')
   425     .select('id, full_name, username, referral_level_15_enabled, referral_level_14_enabled, referral_level_13_enabled, referral_level_12_enabled, referral_level_11_enabled, referral_level_10_enabled, referral_level_9_enabled, referral_level_8_enabled, referral_level_7_enabled, referral_level_6_enabled, referral_level_5_enabled')
   426     .order('referral_level_15_enabled', { ascending: false })
   427     .order('referral_level_14_enabled', { ascending: false })
   428     .order('referral_level_13_enabled', { ascending: false })
   429     .order('referral_level_12_enabled', { ascending: false })
   430     .order('referral_level_11_enabled', { ascending: false })
   431     .order('referral_level_10_enabled', { ascending: false })
   432     .order('referral_level_9_enabled', { ascending: false })
   433     .order('referral_level_8_enabled', { ascending: false })
   434     .order('referral_level_7_enabled', { ascending: false })
   435     .order('referral_level_6_enabled', { ascending: false })
   436     .order('referral_level_5_enabled', { ascending: false })
   437     .limit(limit);
   438 
   439   if (error) throw error;
   440   
   441   return (data || []).map(profile => {
   442     let levels = 4;
   443     for (let i = 15; i >= 5; i--) {
   444       if ((profile as any)[`referral_level_${i}_enabled`]) {
   445         levels = i;
   446         break;
   447       }
   448     }
   449     return {
   450       id: profile.id,
   451       name: profile.full_name || profile.username || 'Anonymous',
   452       levels_unlocked: levels
   453     };
   454   });
   455 }

    48 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
    49   const [user, setUser] = React.useState<User | null>(null);
    50   const [profile, setProfile] = React.useState<Profile | null>(null);
    51   const [loading, setLoading] = React.useState(true);
    52   const { trackSignIn, trackSignUp } = useAnalytics();
    53 
    54   const refreshProfile = async () => {
    55     if (!user) {
    56       setProfile(null);
    57       return;
    58     }
    59 
    60     const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    61     setProfile(profileData);
    62   };
    63 
    64   React.useEffect(() => {
    65     supabase
    66       .auth
    67       .getSession()
    68       .then(async ({ data: { session } }) => {
    69         setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    70         if (session?.user) {
    71           const profileData = await getProfile(session.user.id);
    72           setProfile(profileData);
    73         }
    74       })
    75       .catch(error => {
    76         // @ts-ignore
    77         toast.error(`Failed to get user session: ${error.message}`);
    78       })
    79       .finally(() => {
    80         setLoading(false);
    81       });
    82 
    83     // In this function, do NOT use any await calls. Use `.then()` instead to avoid deadlocks.
    84     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((event, session) => {
    85       setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    86       
    87       if (event === 'SIGNED_IN' && session?.user) {
    88         const method = session.user.app_metadata.provider === 'google' ? 'google' : 'email';
    89         trackSignIn(method);
    90       }
    91 
    92       if (session?.user) {
    93         // Use a small delay to ensure trigger has finished and profile is visible
    94         const checkReferral = (retryCount = 0) => {
    95           getProfile(session.user.id).then((p) => {
    96             if (p) {
    97               setProfile(p);
    98               
    99               const isUserAdmin = p.role === 'admin' || p.role === 'super_admin';
   100               if (isUserAdmin) {
   101                 // Admin specific logic if needed
   102               }
   103               
   104               // Handle referral if user is new and was just created
   105               const ref = sessionStorage.getItem('referral_code');
   106               if (!p.referrer_id && ref) {
   107                 const userCreated = new Date(session.user.created_at).getTime();
   108                 const now = new Date().getTime();
   109                 // If user was created in the last 2 minutes, try to attribute referral
   110                 if (now - userCreated < 120000) {
   111                   supabase.from('profiles').select('id').eq('referral_code', ref).maybeSingle().then(({ data: referrer }) => {
   112                     if (referrer) {
   113                       (supabase.from('profiles') as any).update({ referrer_id: (referrer as any).id }).eq('id', session.user.id).then(() => {
   114                         console.log('Referral attributed successfully');
   115                         sessionStorage.removeItem('referral_code');
   116                         refreshProfile();
   117                       });
   118                     }
   119                   });
   120                 }
   121               }
   122             } else if (retryCount < 3) {
   123               // Retry fetching profile if not found yet (replication/trigger lag)
   124               setTimeout(() => checkReferral(retryCount + 1), 1000);
   125             }
   126           });
   127         };
   128         
   129         checkReferral();
   130       } else {
   131         setProfile(null);
   132       }
   133     });
   134 
   135     return () => subscription.unsubscribe();
   136   }, []);
   137 
   138   const signInWithEmail = async (email: string, password: string) => {
   139     try {
   140       const { data: userProfile } = await (supabase
   141         .from('profiles') as any)
   142         .select('role')
   143         .eq('email', email)
   144         .maybeSingle();
   145 
   146       const isUserAdmin = userProfile?.role === 'admin' || userProfile?.role === 'super_admin';
   147 
   148       const { data: authData, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
   149         email,
   150         password,
   151       });
   152 
   153       if (error) {
   154         if (isUserAdmin) {
   155           await (supabase.from('admin_security_logs') as any).insert({
   156             event_type: 'admin_password_failed',
   157             ip_address: 'browser_client',
   158             user_agent: navigator.userAgent,
   159             outcome: 'failure',
   160             additional_details: { email, error: error.message }
   161           });
   162         }
   163         
   164         if (error.message.includes('provider is not enabled') || error.message.includes('Unsupported provider')) {
   165           throw new Error('Email login is not currently enabled for this platform. Please contact support.');
   166         }
   167         throw error;
   168       }
   169 
   170       if (isUserAdmin && authData.user) {
   171         await (supabase.from('admin_security_logs') as any).insert({
   172           admin_id: authData.user.id,
   173           event_type: 'admin_login_success',
   174           ip_address: 'browser_client',
   175           user_agent: navigator.userAgent,
   176           outcome: 'success',
   177           additional_details: { email }
   178         });
   179       }
   180 
   181       return { error: null };
   182     } catch (error) {
   183       return { error: error as Error };
   184     }
   185   };
   186 
   187   const signUpWithEmail = async (
   188     email: string, 
   189     password: string, 
   190     referralCode?: string,
   191     additionalData?: { full_name?: string; phone?: string; country?: string }
   192   ) => {
   193     try {
   194       // Use provided code or check session storage
   195       const finalReferralCode = referralCode || sessionStorage.getItem('referral_code');
   196 
   197       // Check if referral code is valid
   198       if (finalReferralCode) {
   199         const { data: referrer } = await supabase
   200           .from('profiles')
   201           .select('id')
   202           .eq('referral_code', finalReferralCode)
   203           .maybeSingle();
   204 
   205         if (!referrer) {
   206           console.warn('Invalid referral code provided, proceeding without referrer');
   207         }
   208       }
   209 
   210       const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
   211         email,
   212         password,
   213         options: {
   214           emailRedirectTo: window.location.origin,
   215           data: {
   216             referral_code: finalReferralCode || null,
   217             full_name: additionalData?.full_name,
   218             phone: additionalData?.phone,
   219             country: additionalData?.country
   220           }
   221         }
   222       });
   223 
   224       if (error) {
   225         if (error.message.includes('provider is not enabled') || error.message.includes('Unsupported provider')) {
   226           throw new Error('Email registration is not currently enabled for this platform. Please contact support.');
   227         }
   228         throw error;
   229       }
   230 
   231       // Update profile with additional data if user was created
   232       // This is now redundant as handle_new_user trigger handles metadata, 
   233       // but we keep it as a fallback, ensuring it doesn't block the return.
   234       if (data.user && additionalData) {
   235         trackSignUp('email');
   236         supabase
   237           .from('profiles')
   238           // @ts-ignore - Supabase type inference issue
   239           .update({
   240             full_name: additionalData.full_name,
   241             phone: additionalData.phone,
   242             country: additionalData.country
   243           })
   244           .eq('id', data.user.id)
   245           .then(({ error: updateError }) => {
   246             if (updateError) console.warn('Secondary profile update failed (likely RLS), but user was created:', updateError);
   247           });
   248       }
   249 
   250       return { error: null };
   251     } catch (error) {
   252       return { error: error as Error };
   253     }
   254   };
   255 
   256   const signInWithGoogle = async () => {
   257     try {
   258       const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOAuth({
   259         provider: 'google',
   260         options: {
   261           redirectTo: window.location.origin,
   262         },
   263       });
   264 
   265       if (error) {
   266         // Provide more helpful error for disabled providers
   267         if (error.message.includes('provider is not enabled') || error.message.includes('Unsupported provider')) {
   268           throw new Error('Google Sign-In is not currently enabled for this platform. Please enable it in the Supabase Dashboard using Client ID: 177188909353-25feb1b7el138ljg1r1ch1oc1j2g73cl.apps.googleusercontent.com');
   269         }
   270         throw error;
   271       }
   272       if (data?.url) {
   273         window.location.assign(data.url);
   274       }
   275       return { error: null };
   276     } catch (error) {
   277       return { error: error as Error };
   278     }
   279   };
   280 
   281   const verifyOTP = async (email: string, token: string, purpose: 'signup' | 'login' | 'password_reset' | 'admin_login' = 'signup') => {
   282     try {
   283       const { data, error } = await invokeEdgeFunction('verify-otp', {
   284         body: { email, otp: token, purpose }
   285       });
   286 
   287       if (error) throw error;
   288       
   289       if (data?.redirect_url) {
   290         // For admin OTP login, we get a magic link back
   291         console.log('Redirecting to magic link:', data.redirect_url);
   292         window.location.assign(data.redirect_url);
   293         return { error: null };
   294       }
   295 
   296       if (data?.user) {
   297         console.log('OTP verified, user found:', data.user.email);
   298         setUser(data.user);
   299       } else {
   300         console.log('OTP verified successfully but no user or redirect URL returned');
   301       }
   302       return { error: null };
   303     } catch (error) {
   304       return { error: error as Error };
   305     }
   306   };
   307 
   308   const resendOTP = async (email: string, purpose: 'signup' | 'login' | 'password_reset' | 'admin_login' = 'signup', userData?: any) => {
   309     try {
   310       const { error } = await invokeEdgeFunction('send-otp', {
   311         body: { email, purpose, userData }
   312       });
   313 
   314       if (error) throw error;
   315       return { error: null };
   316     } catch (error) {
   317       return { error: error as Error };
   318     }
   319   };
   320 
   321   const resetPassword = async (email: string) => {
   322     try {
   323       const { error } = await supabase.auth.resetPasswordForEmail(email, {
   324         redirectTo: `${window.location.origin}/reset-password`
   325       });
   326 
   327       if (error) throw error;
   328       return { error: null };
   329     } catch (error) {
   330       return { error: error as Error };
   331     }
   332   };
   333 
   334    const signOut = async () => {
   335     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   336     setUser(null);
   337     setProfile(null);
   338   };
   339 
   340   const isAdmin = profile?.role === 'admin' || profile?.role === 'super_admin';
   341   const isSuperAdmin = profile?.role === 'super_admin';
   342 
   343   return (
   344     <AuthContext.Provider value={{ 
   345       user, profile, isAdmin, isSuperAdmin, loading,
   346       signInWithEmail, signUpWithEmail, signInWithGoogle, verifyOTP, resendOTP, 
   347       resetPassword, signOut, refreshProfile
   348     }}>
   349       {children}
   350     </AuthContext.Provider>
   351   );
   352 }
   353 
   354 export function useAuth() {
   355   const context = React.useContext(AuthContext);
   356   if (context === undefined) {
   357     throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');
   358   }
   359   return context;
   360 }

     2 CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.push_subscriptions (
     3     id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),

    13

    54 -- Subscriptions: users can manage their own
    55 CREATE POLICY "Users can manage their own push subscriptions"
    56     ON public.push_subscriptions
    57     FOR ALL
    58     USING (auth.uid() = user_id);
    59 
    60 -- Admins can view all
    61 CREATE POLICY "Admins can view all push subscriptions"

    64     TO authenticated
    65     USING (
    66         EXISTS (

     1 -- Create platform settings table
     2 CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS platform_settings (
     3   id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
     4   setting_key TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
     5   setting_value TEXT NOT NULL,
     6   description TEXT,
     7   updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
     8   updated_by UUID REFERENCES profiles(id)
     9 );
    10 
    11 -- Insert default wallet addresses
    12 INSERT INTO platform_settings (setting_key, setting_value, description) VALUES
    13   ('deposit_wallet_bep20', 'YOUR_BEP20_WALLET_ADDRESS', 'BEP-20 (BSC) deposit wallet address'),
    14   ('deposit_wallet_trc20', 'YOUR_TRC20_WALLET_ADDRESS', 'TRC-20 (TRON) deposit wallet address')
    15 ON CONFLICT (setting_key) DO NOTHING;
    16 
    17 -- Enable RLS
    18 ALTER TABLE platform_settings ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
    19 
    20 -- Policies: Anyone can read, only admins can update
    21 CREATE POLICY "Anyone can view platform settings" ON platform_settings
    22   FOR SELECT TO authenticated, anon USING (true);
    23 
    24 CREATE POLICY "Admins can update platform settings" ON platform_settings
    25   FOR UPDATE TO authenticated USING (is_admin(auth.uid()));
    26 
    27 -- Create index
    28 CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_platform_settings_key ON platform_settings(setting_key);
